msg:Atour Hotel is common, but five-star Atour is not common!
I had the honor of staying at the five-star Atour Hotel in Wuxi Coast City. This stay left a deep impression on me and I was very satisfied.

First of all, as soon as I entered the hotel lobby, I was attracted by its exquisite and elegant decoration style. The lobby is spacious and bright, and the golden decorations and soft lights complement each other, creating a noble and warm a**osphere. The front desk staff are polite and enthusiastic. Their professional service and kind smiles made me feel the warmth of home instantly.

The room I stayed in is uniquely designed, spacious and reasonably laid out. The room is exquisitely decorated and the furniture is of high quality, giving people a high-quality enjoyment. Especially the beautiful scenery outside the floor-to-ceiling windows, so that I can enjoy the charming coastal scenery every time I wake up, and my mood is particularly happy.

In addition, the hotel's facilities are also very complete. Whether it is the intelligent control system or the high-quality bedding and bathroom facilities, they all show the hotel's ultimate pursuit of details. Especially the spaciousness and comfort of the bathroom, I was fully relaxed and enjoyed during my trip.

In terms of service, Atour Hotel also performed well. From check-in to check-out, the hotel staff provided me with all kinds of help and services warmly and thoughtfully. They not only patiently answered my questions, but also took the initiative to provide some practical travel suggestions, which made me feel the care of home.

Overall, Wuxi Coast City Five-Star Atour Hotel left me with an excellent impression. Whether it is hardware facilities, service quality or stay experience, it is first-class. If you are looking for a high-quality hotel as your travel destination, then I strongly recommend you to stay at Wuxi Coast City Five-Star Atour Hotel, I believe you will have an unforgettable stay experience.

msg:Coastal City Atour Hotel is located in the coastal city area of an urban complex on the shore of Taihu Lake in the south of Wuxi. It is accessible from Exit 7 of Civic Center Station of Metro Line 1, and the traffic is very convenient. The hotel's service is in place and warm and attentive. The room is very clean and a**ospheric. The large floor-to-ceiling windows can enjoy the day and night city view of Taihu New Town, and even the Taihu Lake and Lihu Lake in the distance can be seen. The breakfast is plentiful and delicious. In short, it is a hotel worth staying at with high cost performance. Those who drive by themselves can park their car in Zone F of the Coastal City Underground Garage, and then take the elevator to the hotel lobby on the 36th floor to check in in the direction of the arrow in the hotel office area.
